Big discount this time! The room is large, but there are several problems!
First｜The sound insulation of the roadside room is too poor and very noisy.
Second: I turned off the air conditioning switch very early in the morning, causing the indoor temperature to reach as high as 27 degrees! It makes people very hot and stuffy! It's only after 10 o'clock and the switchboard is turned off for cooling!
Third | It’s best to replace the shampoo and shower gel bottles with small disposable bottles! There are too many cases of unknown things being poured into bottles! There is a hidden danger!
Fourth｜The towels are of good quality! However, it does not absorb water! After taking a shower, it feels cold when I put it on because it doesn't absorb water!
The above comments are supported by pictures! Hope to change it!

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Superior Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in December 2023
info:Solo travelers
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted December 31, 2023
msg:我最近在此住宿，對其留下了深刻的印象。
	1.	地理位置：酒店地理位置十分優越，周圍出行和購物都非常方便。最重要的是房間景觀一絕，從窗外看出去，可以欣賞到美麗的城市風光，讓人心情愉悦。
	2.	早餐：酒店的早餐種類豐富，品質上乘。無論是熱菜、冷盤還是水果，都能滿足各種口味的需求。而且，餐廳的服務也很周到，讓人感覺賓至如歸。
	3.	前廳服務：前廳工作人員非常熱情，給人一種賓至如歸的感覺。工作效率也高，入住和退房手續辦理得非常迅速，沒有浪費我太多時間。
	4.	客房衞生：客房打掃得非常乾淨，床鋪整潔，衞生間也沒有任何異味。房間基礎設施一應俱全，住起來非常舒適。
這是一家令人滿意的酒店，我非常願意推薦給其他人，並期待再次入住。
